name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Suite
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:5 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:As an old five-star hotel in Wuxi, Degen Hotel is indeed in an excellent location and has very good service. I booked 2 superior suites for 2 nights. Because there is only one suite on each floor, the two suites are located on different floors and have different layouts. The entire facility is a bit old, but it is sufficient. It is located in the Chong'an Temple business district, surrounded by shopping malls such as Hang Lung and Great Eastern. You can go out to find food at 10 o'clock at night. It takes only 2 minutes to walk downstairs to Sanyang Plaza. The transportation is extremely convenient. If you travel by car, guests staying in the hotel can park for free in the Huaguang Building parking lot. There is an affordable beverage cabinet on the first floor, which can be purchased by face recognition... The service is also very good. I bought McDonald's on the first night, but accidentally knocked it over in the elevator waiting area on the first floor. I told the front desk with guilt, and someone handled it immediately. They also told the surrounding guests to be careful. In the middle of the night on the first night, my daughter grabbed the quilt, so I called the room service at 5 am to add a quilt, and they responded quickly. Finally, I lost a piece of jade when I checked out. Jade is not worth much, but because it was given by my parents when I was young, it is of great commemorative value to me. I contacted the hotel the next day and helped find it. I arranged for the courier to send it back as soon as possible. Thank you very much... Having said so many good places, there are of course places that can be improved. First, the door handle of Suite 3423 where I stayed was blocked and needed to be turned with force. Second, compared with most star-rated hotels, the buffet breakfast has room for improvement in terms of the variety and taste of the dishes... Overall, the flaws do not cover the merits. As an old star-rated hotel, Degen Hotel is indeed a good choice for Wuxi tourism accommodation

I booked this hotel because it has a gym. After arriving at the hotel, I checked in and went straight to the gym to see what the conditions are. The first feeling when I entered was cold, icy cold. I thought it was normal for the Yangtze River Basin to be a little cold in this season. I quickly turned on all three air conditioners and adjusted them to the highest temperature. I went back to the room to rest and prepared to go down to lift weights for half an hour. Forty minutes later, I went downstairs wearing a vest, shorts and a thin bathrobe from the hotel and started training! I felt something was wrong as soon as I entered. Why was it colder than before? I really felt like I was wearing a down jacket in the north and shivering. I quickly called the front desk at the gym, and the guy at the front desk told me to contact the engineering department immediately. I thought, just wait a while, once the master comes, the hot air will blow, and it won‚Äôt be a big problem. It doesn‚Äôt matter if I wait for ten minutes in the gym and no one comes! My feet are already frozen. Let's go back to the room quickly. By the way, the room temperature in this hotel is not high. It is set to 35 degrees, but the actual temperature is always around 20 degrees. I waited for 40 minutes, but no one answered me. I called the front desk again this time. A girl answered the phone. She told me that the master had checked it and said that the gym had not been used for a long time. The central air conditioner needs time to heat up, which caused the situation just now. I told her that this is not right. No matter how cold the air conditioning pipe is, I turned it on when I came to the hotel. It is still cold after 40 or 50 minutes. I am afraid it is not a problem that the system needs to be preheated? Then, the girl suggested that I go down and take a look. The temperature should be almost up. Since they have checked it and repaired it, I still have doubts in my heart. Facing the desire to lift iron, I embarked on a freezing journey for the second time. This time when I walked into the gym, the fire came up all of a sudden. Not only did it not heat up, but it was even colder than before, freezing cold! I communicated with the front desk again in the ice-cold environment of the gym. I said to the girl, can you take charge of this matter so far? It‚Äôs better to call the manager to talk to me because it‚Äôs too cold here! I booked your hotel because it has a gym. I won‚Äôt exercise today and I want a refund. The answer given by the front desk girl this time was to find the leader and asked me to go back to the room and wait for news. I will call back in 10 minutes. I went back to the room and the phone rang soon. First, the refund was not allowed, but the room type could be upgraded. Second, two heaters had been moved in, and I was asked to exercise in half an hour. I looked at the watch and it was ten o'clock. Half an hour later, it would be half past ten. I was asked to lift weights at half past ten in the evening? I was furious. I said, I don‚Äôt like to exercise at midnight, and I now suspect that it will still be cold there half an hour later.

msg:Mites are everywhere in every corner. I checked in at 10.10 in the morning. After washing, I put on the quilt and found that my skin was a little itchy. I didn't want to move, so I ignored it. At noon, I also had some mite allergies - urticaria. I called the hotel at 12 noon to check the reason for the room. Then check out. At 4 o'clock in the afternoon, erythema began to appear on a large area of ‚Äã‚Äã‚Äã‚Äãthe skin. When I called the hotel, the staff expressed their ignorance and added WeChat. They did not admit that there was any unclean place during the communication. It has been 10 days since we came out and we have been staying in hotels. We have not had such allergic reactions, and allergic reactions are rapid. After the communication was fruitless, we called 110 and 12345 and went to the hotel front desk for processing. The manager never came forward and the hotel staff did not admit any responsibility. After the police's persuasion, the hotel compensated us with 212 yuan for the cost of the pharmacy. We were also disheartened. The city of Wuxi should not be like this! On the evening of the 11th, my condition began to worsen, and I contacted the manager. His attitude was very tough, and the communication was fruitless. Around 10pm on the evening of the 11th, I went to the Dermatology Depar**ent of the First Affiliated Hospital of Suzhou University and it was confirmed that it was measles caused by allergies. After applying the medicine on the 12th, my skin improved. I communicated with the hotel again on the 12th and still did not admit any fault. The review is just for those who have high standards of hygiene to be cautious before entering!
